STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statements of income for the nine months
ended September&nbsp;30, 2004 and the year ended December 31, 2003 have been prepared based on the historical consolidated statements of income of Plains and Nuevo under the assumptions set forth in the accompanying footnotes. All of these
transactions are reflected in Plains&#146; consolidated balance sheet at September 30, 2004. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On May 14, 2004, Plains acquired Nuevo in a stock for stock transaction. Plains issued 36.5 million shares of common stock to Nuevo shareholders and assumed Nuevo&#146;s $150 million of 9<FONT
SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;3</SUP></FONT><FONT SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">8</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000">% Notes, $140 million outstanding under Nuevo&#146;s credit facility and $115 million of TECONs. Under the terms of
the transaction, Nuevo stockholders received 1.765 shares of Plains common stock for each share of Nuevo common stock. This transaction has been accounted for using the purchase method of accounting. The effect of this transaction is reflected in
the Nuevo Merger Adjustments column in the unaudited pro forma combined statements of income. </FONT></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On June 29, 2004, Nuevo (a wholly owned subsidiary of Plains) completed the repurchase of all $150 million of its outstanding 9<FONT
SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;3</SUP></FONT><FONT SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">8</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000">% Notes. Nuevo paid $1,150.08 per $1,000 principal amount of 9<FONT SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;3</SUP></FONT><FONT
SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">8</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000">% Notes tendered (comprising the tender offer price of $1,107.16, plus accrued interest through June 29, 2004 of $22.92, plus the consent payment of
$20.00). The tender offer and consent payment totaled $169.1 million. </FONT></FONT></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT
FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On June 29, 2004, Nuevo completed the redemption of all outstanding $115 million aggregate principal amount of its TECONs for total consideration of $117.0 million. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On June 30, 2004 Plains completed the private placement under Rule 144A and
Regulation S of the Securities Act of 1933 of $250 million in aggregate principal amount of ten year senior unsecured notes. The 7.125% Notes were issued at 99.478% and bear interest at 7.125% with a yield to maturity of 7.2%. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The repurchase of the 9<FONT SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;3</SUP></FONT><FONT
SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">8</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000"> % Notes, the redemption of the TECONs and the issuance of the 7.125% Notes are referred to herein as the Recapitalization Transactions and are reflected
in the Recapitalization Adjustments column in the unaudited pro forma combined statements of income. </FONT></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On April 8, 2004 Nuevo, together with its wholly owned subsidiary Nuevo International Inc., entered into
a definitive agreement to sell Nuevo&#146;s operations offshore The Republic of Congo via the sale of the stock of Nuevo&#146;s subsidiaries that hold the Congo properties. The transaction was consummated on July 30, 2004. The pro forma effects of
that transaction on Nuevo&#146;s historical consolidated statements of income is discussed in Note&nbsp;2 to the pro forma combined financial statements. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The pro forma effects on Plains&#146; consolidated statement of income for the year ended December 31, 2003 of Plains&#146; acquisition of 3TEC, which was
completed on June 4, 2003, and Plains&#146; issuance of $75 million of 8.75% senior subordinated notes on May 30, 2003 are presented in Note 5 to the pro forma combined financial statements. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statement of income for the nine months
ended September 30, 2004 presents the pro forma effects of the merger of Plains and Nuevo, the Recapitalization Transactions and the sale of Nuevo&#146;s Congo operations as though such transactions occurred on January 1, 2004. The unaudited pro
forma combined statement of income for the year ended December 31, 2003 assume such transactions, together with Plains acquisition of 3TEC and the issuance of the 8.75% Notes occurred on January 1, 2003. Plains believes the assumptions used provide
a reasonable basis for presenting the significant effects directly attributable to such transactions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Income from continuing operations for the nine months ended September 30, 2004 and the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2003 has been reduced by $22.7 million
and $12.6 million, respectively, for losses on early extinguishment of debt. Approximately $19.7 million of the debt extinguishment loss in the 2004 period is related to the Recapitalization Transactions. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">In February 2004 Nuevo redeemed the $75 million balance outstanding of its
9.5% Senior Subordinated Notes due June 1, 2008 at 104.75%. The redemption was funded by proceeds from real estate sales and bank debt. We estimate the redemption results in annual interest expense savings of approximately $6 million. The effect of
the redemption is not reflected as a pro forma adjustment to the historical data. In addition, we have not reflected as an adjustment to the historical data annual cost savings of approximately $20 million that we expect to result from the merger
with Nuevo. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statements of
income do not purport to represent what Plains results of operations would have been if such transactions had occurred on such dates. The unaudited pro forma combined statements of income should be read in conjunction with the Quarterly Report on
Form 10-Q of Plains for the nine months ended September 30, 2004, the Annual Report on Form 10-K of Plains for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2003 (as amended), the Consolidated Financial Statements of 3TEC included in Plains&#146; Registration
Statement on Form S-4 (No. 333-108407) filed August 29, 2003, the Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q of Nuevo for the three months ended March 31, 2004 and the Annual Report on Form 10-K of Nuevo for the year ended December 31, 2003. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

pro forma effect of: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>

STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR>
<TD WIDTH="4%"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Plains&#146; issuance of $75 million of 8.75% Senior Subordinated Notes (the &#147;8.75% Notes&#148;) on May 30, 2003. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statements of income for the nine months
ended September 30, 2004 and the year ended December 31, 2003 have been prepared based on the historical consolidated statements of income of Plains and Nuevo under the assumptions set forth herein. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The effect of the merger of Plains and Nuevo is reflected in the Nuevo Merger
Adjustments column in the unaudited pro forma combined statements of income. The repurchase of the 9<FONT SIZE="1"><SUP>&nbsp;3</SUP></FONT><FONT SIZE="2">/</FONT><FONT SIZE="1">8</FONT><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2" COLOR="#000000"> % Notes,
the redemption of the TECONs and the issuance of the 7.125% Notes are referred to herein as the Recapitalization Transactions and are reflected in the Recapitalization Adjustments column in the unaudited pro forma combined statements of income.
</FONT></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statement of income
for the nine months ended September 30, 2004 presents the pro forma effects of the merger of Plains and Nuevo, the Recapitalization Transactions and the sale of Nuevo&#146;s Congo operations as though such transactions occurred on January 1, 2004.
The unaudited pro forma combined statement of income for the year ended December 31, 2003 assume such transactions, together with Plains acquisition of 3TEC and the issuance of the 8.75% Notes occurred on January 1, 2003. Plains believes the
assumptions used provide a reasonable basis for presenting the significant effects directly attributable to such transactions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The merger with Nuevo has been accounted for using the purchase method of accounting for business combinations. Under the purchase method of accounting,
Nuevo&#146;s assets and liabilities acquired or assumed are revalued and recorded at their estimated fair values. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Plains follows the full cost method of accounting for oil and gas properties while Nuevo follows the successful efforts method of accounting. Certain
costs that are capitalized under the full cost method are expensed under the successful efforts method. These costs consist primarily of costs associated with unsuccessful exploration drilling, geological and geophysical costs and general and
administrative costs associated with acquisition, exploration, exploitation and development activities. Under full cost accounting proceeds from the sale of oil and gas properties are reflected as reductions to capitalized costs unless such sales
involve a significant change in the relationship between costs and the estimated value of proved reserves, in which case a gain or loss is recognized. Pro forma entries include the reclassification of certain of these items to conform Nuevo&#146;s
accounting to the full cost method. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NOTE 2&#151;SALE OF NUEVO CONGO
OPERATIONS </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On April 8, 2004 Nuevo, together with its
wholly owned subsidiary Nuevo International Inc., entered into a definitive agreement to sell Nuevo&#146;s operations offshore The Republic of Congo via the sale of the stock of </FONT>
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">5 </FONT></P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" COLOR="#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
<h5 align="left"><a href="#toc">Table of Contents</a></h5>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px">
<FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Nuevo&#146;s subsidiaries that hold the Congo properties. The sale was consummated on July 30, 2004. Nuevo&#146;s historical income from continuing
operations for the period from January 1 to May 13, 2004 and the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2003 have been adjusted to reflect the sale of such operations effective January 1 of the period presented. Nuevo&#146;s historical income from continuing
operations for the period January 1 to May 13, 2004 was reduced by $1.0 million including amounts related to: revenues&#151;$12.7 million, production expenses&#151;$3.9 million, depreciation, depletion, amortization and accretion&#151;$1.6 million
and income tax expense&#151;$6.2 million. Nuevo&#146;s historical income from continuing operations for the year ended December 31, 2003 was reduced by $23.0 million including amounts related to: revenues&#151;$42.8 million, production
expenses&#151;$10.5 million, depreciation, depletion, amortization and accretion&#151;$5.8 million and income tax expense&#151;$3.5 million. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NOTE 3&#151;PRO FORMA ADJUSTMENTS RELATED TO THE MERGER </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma statements of income include the following adjustments: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(a) Reclassification of certain Nuevo revenue/expense items to conform to the Plains presentation.
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(b) Reflects the reversal of Nuevo historical
exploration costs that are expensed under the successful efforts methods of accounting and are capitalized under the full cost method of accounting. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(c) Reflects the reversal of Nuevo&#146;s merger-related costs. These costs include investment banking, legal, accounting, severance
payments to Nuevo management and an $8.5 million non-cash charge related to restricted stock that vested as a result of the merger. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(d) Reflects the reversal of the gain on disposition of oil and gas properties and assets held for sale. Under full cost accounting,
proceeds from the sale of oil and gas properties are accounted for as reductions to capitalized costs unless such sales involve a significant change in the relationship between costs and the estimated value of proved reserves, in which case a gain
or loss is recognized. The remaining gain on disposition of property relates to sales of non-oil and gas properties. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(e) Adjusts depreciation, depletion, amortization and accretion expense based on the fair value allocated to oil and gas properties. Pro
forma depreciation, depletion and amortization for the combined company is calculated using the unit of production method based on the oil and gas property costs, reserve volumes and future development and abandonment costs of the combined
companies. The pro forma depreciation, depletion and amortization rate for oil and gas properties subject to amortization is $5.93 per barrel of oil equivalent. Accretion expense has been adjusted to reflect Plains&#146; credit adjusted risk free
interest rate and other assumptions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">(f)
Adjusts historical interest expense for the effect of debt assumed and incurred in connection with the merger and interest capitalized on oil and gas properties not subject to amortization of $4.2 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2004
and $8.9 million for the year ended December 31, 2003. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman"
SIZE="2">(g) Reflects the adjustment of income tax expense based on a post-merger effective rate of approximately 37% (42% for the year ended December 31, 2003 including return to provision adjustments included in Plains&#146; historical income tax
expense for the period). </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px" ALIGN="center"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">6 </FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2"><B>NOTE 4&#151;EARNINGS PER SHARE </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:-6px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Earnings per share for the nine months ended September 30, 2004 and the year ended December 31, 2003 have been calculated

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">Plains issuance of $75 million of 8.75% senior subordinated notes on May 30, 2003. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT
SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">On June 4, 2003 Plains acquired 3TEC for approximately $312.9 million in cash and common stock plus $90.0 million to retire
outstanding debt and $14.7 million to retire outstanding 3TEC preferred stock. Under the terms of the agreement 3TEC stockholders received $8.50 in cash and 0.85 shares of our common stock for each share of 3TEC common stock. This transaction has
been accounted for using the purchase method of accounting. The effect of this transaction is reflected in the 3TEC Merger Adjustments in the unaudited pro forma consolidated statements of income. </FONT></P> <P
STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px; text-indent:4%"><FONT FACE="Times New Roman" SIZE="2">The unaudited pro forma combined statement of income for the year ended
December 31, 2003 assumes the 3TEC merger transactions and the $75 million notes offering occurred on January 1, 2003. Plains believes the assumptions used provide a reasonable basis for presenting the significant effects directly attributable to
such transactions. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:0px"><FONT SIZE="1">&nbsp;</FONT></P>
